# TwVillage

## Get data

- Get one data:
```
(your link)/twVillage/(Key)/
```

- Get all data:
```
(your link)/twVillage/
```

- For example, if you use `http://localhost:8000/twVillage/100060097/`, you will get geojson of `台中市/太平區/中興里`.
